* Dictionary *
session:		session #
period:		period #
id:			id #
female:		= 1 if male, 0 o/w
major:		major
group:		identifies subjects that were grouped together
sub_session:	identifies subjects that could be matched together in a session
would_pay:		what the subject offered to pay
would_receive:	what the partner offered to pay
game:			game
exogenous:		= 1 if transfered were determine exogenously, 0 o/w
cooperate:		= 1 if cooperated, 0 o/w
row:			= 1 for row players, 0 o/w
transfer:		= 1 if subjects were in a session where they could offer transfers, 0 o/w
**************
